Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you treat the disease of swollen stomach with a poultice, and the medicine comes out quickly, continue to apply it until it is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are festered or abscessed, the poultice should be as subtle as for an infant;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	And this is the form of the subtle enema when the skin is tightened:
des plaies	for the wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have already said in the previous section about the treatment of wounds; now we shall tell you the treatments for hands and medicines, according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made of, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and for how they were made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	Wounds are made by the thrust of a spear, cut of sword and knife, or lance, club, arrow, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or according to the rules of the body, as in a wound that falls on the neck, or the head, or the side, or the belly, or the liver, and similar limbs;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the cure for each wound, and I will begin with simple wounds of the head, for it will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say when a simple wound comes or a head, and the bone is not broken, be careful if it is from arrow shot or similar things, and the skin is torn completely and the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and if there is doubt about the abscess rising: make it drain from the head itself immediately whether blood comes from the wound, or on the contrary drain from the damaged area;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	empty the patient of excessive wine and heavy foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if it does not want to heal, reduce its flesh, and let it drink no wine, nor eat any meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And put on the wound, if an abscess grows there, wool dampened in rose oil only, or in styptic wine.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if there is no hot abscess, put on the fresh wound with all its blood, which is not moving due to air, and the following powder:   ...
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if the arrow has moved it (the wound), put some ointments on it until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large, such as the size of a sword and similar, and the lips cannot be brought together by tension, then bring them together by stitching, as I will say about abdominal wounds, of the stitching.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is open to the bone, and pitted, and does not hold but only a little, then close it; then treat the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh in place of skin.
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	And command the patient to eat large foods, such as heads and cooked wheat, as well as peas and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	If you find or see rotten flesh without reaching the bone, strike the entire rotten area and throw it away, then heal it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	If there is an artery in the wound or vein that cannot be stopped with medicine, cut it and find where the artery is dislocated. Tie it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	If that does not help, cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, the treatment is light: it is that you put this powder on it which will harden as soon as the arsenic moves it.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	The manner of the powder is: take incense one part; dragon's blood 2 parts; live coal 4 parts, and grind them finely.
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	and treat the wound, press it firmly so that it drains well and unites with all its blood.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And then tie it up well, and leave it to heal without being untied, if it does not swell; for one does not remove the medicine until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	Occasionally, one does this with alum only, when there is no incense or dragon's blood, but the sore has not moved.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the sore has moved itself, it must not be put on this powder.
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	But place on some digested ointments, or poultices made from flour of barley boiled with water and honey, until it exudes pus;
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then heal it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if a bone fracture comes with the wound, and it is small, extract it with subtle forceps;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	And I will tell you after the fractures of the head.
de la plaie dou col	of the wound on the neck   (or "wounds of the neck")
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If a wound occurs on the neck and it is simple (without complication), it does not differ from that of the head, but if the nerves of the neck or the arteries are severed.   (or "If a wound comes about or on the neck and it is simple without any difference with that of the head, but if the nerves or arteries of the neck are severed.")
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nose, there is no other remedy but to let it heal and not put anything restricting, for it harms the nose and causes it to recede.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And not to put anything cold on the wound, for the substance of the nose is cold, and its continuation with the brain which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but let the medicine be warm, such as warm water washed in sweet oil and mixed with rose oil, and boiled water washed similarly in sweet oil.
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	And other stones of similar kind in this manner, and always moist.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the wound is large, tie it with strips, then treat it until it heals.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and pus-filled, pierce or make an incision lower down.   \] Et s’il en a plusieurs, puis les cercle par une corsse en longueur et largeur convenables, si com li maistre me l'a dit;
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the arteries are cut, bleeding will follow, so tie off the wound, and cauterization is necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if the spine of the throat or the veins are cut, the conduct should be kept so that the meat (flesh) can go through.
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	If the vein is on the throat's neck, do not touch the throat but reset it according to its natural shape.
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then let it heal naturally, and leave it for some days, then treat with warm herbs until it is healed.
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	And if the wound presses on the bone, cut it.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	And if there are pieces of bone, pull them all out as you can, and those that you cannot pull out, leave until the wound heals.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	make the opening narrow and even.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, sprinkle powder on it as I have said.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and it has a fistula, treat it as I said in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of a wound from a lance or sword
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If the wound is from a lance or sword and it is deep, check if it is breathing quickly; then know that the wound is deadly.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not healed, and it is fresh with all its blood, do not put the powder on it immediately nor bind it for the blood which will dissolve completely.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	return to the heart, and cut open the patient;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but apply attracting ointment, and bind it twice a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you don't have ointment, put old cotton on the wound to draw out moisture,
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	And make the patient sleep on the wound for 3 or 4 days, or more.
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	If it does not cause spasm or bad trembling of the heart nor drawing of the entrails;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see good signs, you will know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then remove the tents (bandages) and other treatments, once it is healed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	If it cannot heal and open, then know that there is a fistula; treat it as appropriate.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	If the wound is from a sword or knife cut, and it is simple, deeper or on the back, then treat what is in front of it.
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	If it is large, sew it up; if it is small, powder it and if it has reached the bone and taken pieces of it, whether the wound or the openings are forced, treat them.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	And if [the wounds] are not drained, let them drain by themselves, align the extractions.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds on other limbs, the judgement is as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	The rupture of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The ruptures of the belly are great and medium-sized and small.
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From the large wound, sometimes the intestines or the intestinal nerves jump out, due to which the introduction of them;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	and stitching is more difficult, and sometimes a small wound is worse than a large one.
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because it is better to push the intestines back in, if not from end to end;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	because the intestines swell soon when they feel the cold, so push them back more gently.
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And because it is more necessary to heal the mother's wound, it is moved (the intestines) back to their place in her, rather than in others (two).
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	Know that the cut of the belly follows four ways:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	The first two common cuts occur in the incision of the abdomen,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	The other cuts in the body and two other specific cuts are common to other wounds.
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And all of them are more suitable with a stitch from the belly, and I shall say each one and declare it.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	If the wound is small, and nothing from the intestines protrudes,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	And the groin area is difficult to reset, which is one of the two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	For the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	For because the intestines are swollen by cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, heat it in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	Moisten a sponge or a linen cloth only with cold water.
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	cook in cold squill and cyperus and spike (a plant species)
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and open the intestine until the inflammation is removed;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And at times, this wine restraining makes it swell as if to burst open.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	When you see the distension spreading, soften the intestines with water or milk and have them cooked.
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	for this is the reason for the intestines to close up little by little;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter, they make a small wound with the instrument used to cut hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first remedy is to apply leeches.
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	we should not cut it unless there is great necessity.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	And this is the instrument to cut through:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	Cut inside the hollow part and do not split, check the shape here:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is opened up, and the intestines leap out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	If you push it back in its natural shape into its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	If you have the power, for it is worth trying.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is wide and located in the lower abdomen,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	you must make the patient lie on their back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and raise their legs higher than their head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it is in the part below the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	then place the head and the buttocks higher than the parts below.
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and similarly if the hernia of the belly is in one of the two parts
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	then put your attention on the fact that the affected part should be higher than the other.
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus, it should be administered as I say for large and medium wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For small wounds use what is prepared.
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then take a compassionate assistant with one hand holding the whole wound with his hand,
et assemble les levres;	And gather the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	And this is the common method of suturing;
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and take a needle or more, according to the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave at the top of the wound a distance of one finger's space, and insert a needle with a single thread of strong filament.
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	And pierce the two joints of the chest with the two joints of the sawbones.
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is beneath the skin inside, as long as you make it pierce from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and put together the two joints of the sawbones four together;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then tighten a double thread around the awl of two parts,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	Then assemble the two heads of the wound facing each other,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and leave one space, and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie the thread as you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and continue doing this with the number of needles needed,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until the entire wound is held in place;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and let the needles be medium-sized, neither too thin nor thick,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because fine needles cut all the fat, while too thick ones cannot enter well;
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	because they must be amputated
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and it is not advisable to push the needles too deeply into the flesh and skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	that they do not cut and open a wound before the joint.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	then cut the joints with needles so that they do not hurt the patient while sleeping.
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	And he places bands or cloths on the head of arrows to keep them still.
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and let it stay until the wound is sutured.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this method of suturing arrows is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because it strengthens an arrow or two.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitch is common.
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and you assemble the two shoulder blades with the two ribs together with a needle, having one strong medium thread.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have pierced all four of them together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	If you straighten the needle at the part where you have started, in the manner as they often sew cloths;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and put space between each stitch the thickness of a small egg;
ceste costure sevent li home,	this stitching heals the man;
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sewed a wound that a man had in his belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	Who was wounded by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound is more than one palm wide,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and it exposes the intestines about two palms in length,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and the wound was in the abdomen.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I returned the intestine as it had been twenty-four hours earlier,
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	and the wound was sewn up for fifteen days, and healed, and became healthy.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged that he would die, and it was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and did not heal him with medicine, for I was in one place where there was none found, nor any medicines;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	And place old cotton above the wound twice a day, and wash it with honey water until it becomes clean.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	Then I will tell you the two proper ways of sewing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle and insert it from the outside part to inside.
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	When it has pierced the heart directly, if the key of the lock is inside the sheep's hide or cost [object] where you have inserted the needle,
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and make it pierce from the inside to the outside until it appears there.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and the understanding of this stitching is that you sew as the tailor does with leather.
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and that you leave one side of the sheep's hide open at first, and close it from the other side once the stitching is completely finished.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of suturing, which Galen calls specifically,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	is like anyone who brings together the two parts naturally,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and apply one of the edges of the skin to the other edge, in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	insert a needle or the edge of the mirror nearby and pierce only that spot,
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	And let the two cheeks of the shoulder rest.
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	Then turn the needle and make it pierce from the outer part until within.
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	two cheeks of the shoulder
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Then pierce one and the other from the outer part until within, in the two other cheeks that are on the opposite side of the chest bone.
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And it is the moistened manner of stitching, and it is the most common.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen said this word, and no one can deny it,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	One must sew the belly with two needles, having thread in each one;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and should one drive one needle from one side, and the other from the other, in the manner of those who sew leather garments.
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	And know that when the rupture is within the abdomen,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	then the stitching of the wound in the abdomen is more severe than in other parts of the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgement of the wound is like the judgement of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it is that when you open the fresh wound with all its blood, just as the arrow has moved it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	If one reinstates the intestine and its casing, then place powder stimulating heat on top.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if it has moved the arrow, place any salve that is present until the wound heals.
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and clean the threads and tie them together with sutures and the needle.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat the wound as others, until it is healed.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	And if you have no medicine, put (something) on it as soon as it begins to emit pus, old cotton.
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and move it two times a day until it is drained.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you do not need any other medicine in many cases where the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound might cause spread to the main members,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	It is necessary that you soak linen lightly in warm oil or rose oil,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it around the affected areas, and underneath the blisters.
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	if there is pain or boils in the belly, and it happens many times,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	if the enemas with black wine are too hot, and especially if the boils come up to the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And pierce within, and know that when it is the large intestines, it is easier to heal than the small ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine called "jeun" cannot heal when perforated,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	and it is due to the planting of worms in them, and the subtlety of the entire body, and the proximity of its nature to nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the herb jumps from the wound, place it back as with the intestines, while it is still fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	And if it is old and turned black, you must cauterize the black area where blood flow should not come.
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	For there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	Then grip that which is between the ligament,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	And hang the two heads suspended from the part below the wound until it opens up to align the extraction, as the bones fall, and the wound bows.
de la routure dou boueil	of the swelling of the boil
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are round and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	If it can be restored in some men, [this refers to] dislocated limbs.
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I have seen a man pierced or wounded with a lance;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach.
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and became swollen and turned into a fistula, with emission and windiness.
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I applied a cure according to what I knew, and did not stop refining until it was healed, and the limbs were sewn together.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw the patient being sewn up, I feared that he had an ailment in his belly;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and he had no illness, but remained in better condition, with food and drink.
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	And they said to any experimenters that when it has a small wound in the intestine, it should be tied in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take thick thread, then gather together the lips of the wound.
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the thread has passed through the mouth, place it on the two lips,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	so that it draws the mouth outwards.
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	And then hold the head (of the patient) firmly so it cannot dislocate.
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	Then put another plaster after in this manner as before, until the wound is completely healed.
et cout la plaie.	and dress the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If the head becomes inflamed in the intestines, it does not cause any harm to the patient.
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	And it can be tied with a fine thread from the intestine of an animal.
en teil maniere:	in this manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take the head of this thread made from the intestine that is very sharp.
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	then tie it to the head of this thread with a fine linen cord.
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Then thread the wire through the needle, sew up the intestine, and tie it in the wound.
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	And this method of stitching sores is not without fear and hope.
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	If the wound is large and wide, especially when it is in one of the small intestines, there is no remedy or health, unless through subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of fistula or that it be.
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	All wounds or abscesses, when they mature, are universally called "fistula".
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	and similarly when it is filled and bursts open.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And a fistula is according to the truth, a hard and white node, where there is no pain,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and it is as swollen as the feather of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	And sometimes clear and other times thick bend.
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	Sometimes shallow, and other times quite deep.
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	And I have spoken of it in the division of wounds, that any wound that is not healed and there is no flesh,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	This is only by one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	It is to be known, by the small amount of blood or heart. (translation)
ou por sa malice;	or for its ill nature; (translation)
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is hard flesh within it, above the lips, which does not allow flesh to grow. (translation)
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or if there is too much pus. (translation)
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	When the limb is broken, and the matter is of bad quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	when the medicine is not good in the cure;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	because the corruption is manner of pestilence;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	because in the region, digestion is slow, and health slows down and declines by nature.
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	Or there are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	And I have already shown all these causes, and the signs, and the cures of medicines in the division.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	And I must tell you the cure for a fistula that is made by manual work.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that a fistula occurs in all members of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	for there are fistulas that come from large veins, and arteries, and nerves.
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or in the bladder, or intestines, or bladder, or any of the ribs.
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	or in the spine of the back, or in any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	And if it affects the property of the main member, and similar joints.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all these fistulas that are in this manner are grave healing, and there is nothing but labor and ignorance.
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	And if there is any fistula that does not go down to the level I have mentioned, and you are confident of the cure,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	and you see it recognized, if it is straight, take a tent of wax or iron, and pierce it.
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	And if the fistula is twisted, seek a thin probe to straighten it.
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	because the probe bends due to twisting;
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	and if the fistula has many holes that you cannot probe with thin probes,
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	if you are to use the clyster (enema) through one of the holes,
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	For moisture is cut from one place to another, and it is purified.
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then seek out cautiously within your power, whether there is bone or nerve, and whether it is closed completely.
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	ask the patient carefully about the pain they feel when pressed by your hand, and where they feel it.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	and when you truly know where it is, and whether it is far from a joint, nerve, artery or vein.
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	or in any of the joints I have mentioned, if the shoulder follows what I have said,
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and break the fracture and corrupt bones that are within;
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	then heal it until it is healed,
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	and if the fistula is well drilled in a straight line, you must cut through to the bone, as much as possible,
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	Then he puts dampened plasters in the medication, and pushes them to the head of the fistula.
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	until the medication corrodes the excess that remains at the bottom;
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then he puts healing ointments in clean jars, while they are still clean;
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	and if they are not clean by this means, then cauterize them as we have said;
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	And if the bone is corrupted by a fistula, strike it.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If neither veins nor nerves trouble or principal limbs, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	And if the bone is exposed and there is corruption and blackness, scrape it until all corruption is removed,
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then heal the harmful things while it is healthy;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	and if it is not healthy, then render it soft as before,
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	know that you are not yet at the fountain:
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	if you discover and seek until you reach the bottom,
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	And remove all corruption, then reset its place.
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is thus healed, that is good.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If not, know that the corruption is too deep, that you cannot reach it.
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	if there is no other device but the natural rest.
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	And if there is a small bone corrupted, and you can draw it with pliers,
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	if the extraction is possible using an instrument,
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	And if there are multiple bones, remove all of them, do not leave any one.
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	and if moisture opposes you and there is no mistake or fear,
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	If hot and moist and fat, and deliver the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	And if you cannot remove them within an hour, put on the wound something irritating like mustard.
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	and leave it until the flesh is purged around the bones.
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	and then they will more easily remove the bones;
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	And if it is a large bone, such as the leg or thigh,
si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee,	and press only the corruption so that the blackness is completely removed.
puis restoure la plaie;	then restore the wound;
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	and if there is a large part of the corruption that reaches the bone marrow;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	If it must be cut and covered up until corruption sets in, then heal it as long as it is healed.
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint .i. home en sa jambe,	And I will tell you about a fistula that occurs on one man's leg.
si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	Take it as an example and help in your work.
Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	A young man of about thirty years had a pain in his leg due to a cause that came from within his body.
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	As long as the matter came to the leg, and was swollen with a large abscess, and there was no reason to open it;
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri,	but they pierced it repeatedly out of folly, so that the abscesses opened up.
et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	and they discharged a lot of matter, and it became a fistula, and much pus came out that made them all weak and full of moisture in the body.
et maint mire i mirent cure entor .ij. ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains,	and many people applied treatment for two years without any skilled hand in medicine.
tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit,	As long as I was called, and saw his leg and the medicines with which he was being treated,
et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	and that which ran through the wounds with great pain.
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	The young man's body turned red, and he had a yellow complexion.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus,	I made a tent over one of the wounds, and then searched all the wounds,
et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	And I found that they come against each other from all parts of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os,	Then I quickly went to one wound and cut into it until I discovered a part of the bone,
et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	And I found it corrupted and pierced through, and the corruption reached down to the bone within;
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I appeared to be that which was corrupt in the bone, and I thought there was no other corruption except for what I left.
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	And began to heal the wound with salty medicines for a long time, but could not suture.
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant,	and then I reinforced it, and uncovered the bone as before,
et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	And I found continuous corruption in the bone, and I removed it, and then I left it to heal, and afterwards I tried to mend the joint.
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole,	but I could not as I wrapped a palm of bone around it and pull it away completely from its socket.
puis le restourai de medicines; et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment,	then I restored it with medicine; and it healed and mended quickly.
et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir,	and there was no need to start the work again except for the weakness of the patient who could not endure it.
et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	And because of the fear of death he had for him.
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement,	For the evacuation of blood often occurred, but he was completely cured.
et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	and a hard cyst grew in the place of the bone, and was of good condition and had no harm or opposite effect at all, neither in the air nor in coming.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if any bone is broken in any part of the body, it must be treated in this manner:
pren .i. liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert,	Take a ligature (or thread), and hold it at the head of the open bone.
et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	And command someone to stretch it upward;
et met .i. autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os,	And take another thicker thread of linen and tie it above the cartilage that is on top of the bone,
et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz,	And stretch the head so that you pull the corrupt cartilage downwards,
et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	And uncover the flesh on the place where you want to be, let the flesh not bleed.
et met .i. tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	And put a splint or a plank under the bone to cover the corrupt flesh.
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	It must be as much as one can see and feel the corruption, and it should be done again.
Et se li os est corrumpus, et n’apert mie, et li corruptions est en mileu ou en une partie,	And if the bone is corrupt but does not open, and the corruption is in the middle or a part of it,
si descuevre la char toute; puis met .i. tison desoz,	If you uncover the flesh completely; then put one iron pin underneath.
et puis soie des l’une partie a l’autre la corruption, et soit li soieure dou lonc de la corruption .i. poc, si com nos avons dit;	and let the corruption from one part to another be covered with silk, and let the silk be the same length as the corruption (as we have said);
et se li corruptions est en la jointure, si cope la jointure corrumpue, et soie l’os ou elle contient de l’autre part;	if the corruption is in a joint, cover the corrupted joint and let the bone on the other side be visible;
et se li corruptions est en la continuation des .ij. jointes, si n’i a autre angien que dou coper;	if the corruption is between two joints, then it should only be covered (with something).
et se li corruptions est ou poignil de la main, ou ou poignil dou piet, si est mout fort celle chose,	And if the corruption is at the end of the hand, or at the heel of the foot, it is very serious.
mais toutevoie il covient que tu enquieres celle corrosion, coment elle t’apert;	but it is necessary that you investigate this corruption, how it opened up;
et la mundifie en toutes les manieres que tu pues, mais que li voine ou li nerf ne te faicent contraire;	and cleanse it in every way possible, but ensure the vein or nerve does not oppose you;
et saiches que li incisoire et les soies por coper ces os sont maintes, selonc l’assise des os et l’aparance d’ous,	and know that the incision and the needles for covering these bones are many, according to the location of the bone and its appearance.
et lor grossece et lor subtiliteit, et lor grandor et lor petitece, et lor duresce;	And their thickness and subtlety, and their largeness and smallness, and their hardness;
et por ceu covient il apareillier a chescune semblance d’ovraige son estrument;	for this reason it is necessary to prepare an instrument suitable for each type of work.
et saiches que l’uevre te moustrera l’estrument dont tu avras mestier, selonc la conissance de cest art,	and know that the work will show you the tool you need, according to the knowledge of this art,
et le tesmoignaige des manieres des maladies;	the testimony of the ways of diseases;
si porpense l’estrument dont tu as mestier selonc ceu qu’il le covient.	If one considers the tool required according to what is necessary for it.
dou feu	The fire
Li chiés porrissent ou par cause dedens, ou par cause defuer;	The head may dislocate either from within or from outside;
et quant tu avras medicinee celle corrosion par la cure des medicines, et il ne profitent mie,	and when you have treated that corruption with medicine and the treatment does not work,
si covient coper celui membre jusques au leu ou li corrosion vient,	It is necessary to cover that member up to the level where corruption comes.
si que li malaides eschaipe par ceu de la mort, ou par la malice, qui est plus grans, de la defaute dou membre;	If the patient shivers because of death or due to greater evil from the member's failure.
et li signes si est que li membres devient noir, si qu’il semble qu’il soit ars dou feu,	And the signs are that the member turns black as if it were burned by fire,
et porrist aprés la noiror, puis va celle corrosions de membre em membre,	And afterwards, the blackness spreads, then comes the corruption of one member to another.
et prent par tout le cors; si te haste dou coper,	And takes hold of the whole body; hasten to cover it.
et se c’est par la percussion d’aucunes venimouses bestes, si com scorpion de mer et wivre et semblans,	and if it is by the strike of some venomous beasts such as sea scorpions and vipers and similar,
se li corrosion est au chief dou doi, si le cope, et ne li doner mie espaice de venir jusc’a la main.	if the corruption is at the head of the finger, strike it and do not give it any space to come up to the hand.
Et s’elle vient jusc’a la main, si la cope a la jointe, si que la corrosion ne viegne jusc’a bras;	If it comes up to the hand, strike at the joint so that the corruption does not come up to the arm;
et s’elle vient au bras, si le cope au coute; et s’elle passe le coute, c’est li mors,	And if it comes to the arm, strike at the bone; and if it passes the bone, it is death,
et n’i vaut amenistremens fuers que li quantitez de sa vertut;	and nothing else is needed but the quantity of its virtue;
et tot ensi fai quant li corrosion vient ou piet: s’elle vient en la premiere jointe, si la cope aprés l’autre jointe;	and do as follows when the corrosion comes or piety: if it comes in the first joint, then strike after the other joint;
et s’elle vient ou piet, si cope tout le piet;	and if it comes to piety, strike all of it;
et s’elle monte en la jambe, si cope a la jointure dou genoil;	And if it moves up into the leg, strike at the knee joint.
et s’elle vient desus le genoil, si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier le malaide a mort;	If it comes above the thigh, there is no other remedy for the patient but to kill him.
et li maniere dou coper ou dou soier le membre si est que tu le lie desus et desoz,	The manner of covering or healing the member is that you tie it above and below,
et estende uns menistres l’un des liiens aval, et uns autres ministres l’autre liien amont,	and extend one minister below the tie, and another minister above it.
et tu dessevre la char qui est entre les .ij. liiens a .i. spatumile large, tant que li os soit descovers;	And you sever the flesh that is between the two ligaments at one space of about a thumb's width wide, while the bone is exposed;
puis le cope ou soie, et met de chescune part .i. drapeil de lin, si que li soie ne touche le leu sain,	then put the copper or silk, and place one linen cloth on each side, so that the silk does not touch the healthy area,
et viegne au malaide autre lesion et aposteme chaus.	and another wound or abscess occurs on the patient;
Et se decorremens de sanc vient quant tu oevres, si cauterize le leu hastanment,	And when bleeding occurs as you work, quickly cauterize the area.
ou tu met sus aucunes poudres restraignans; puis revien a ta medicine tant qu’elle soit acomplie,	and apply some powders that restrain [the bleeding]; then return to your medication until it is completed.
puis lie le membre navreit d’un liien covenauble, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then bind the limb with a tight bandage and let it heal until it is sound;
et je te conterai k’il avint a .i. home en som piet:	and I will tell you about what happened to one man in a similar situation:
il li avint une noiror qui sembloit arsure de feu,	It happened to him a blackness resembling burned flesh,
et celle corrosion vint premier en son doi dou piet, tant qu’elle porprist tout le piet;	and that corrosion began first on his tooth root, until it ate through all the tooth;
et quant li hons vit la corrosion, si se hasta de coper le piet, et fut sanez;	and when the man saw the corrosion, he pierced the tooth with a copper instrument, and became healthy;
et lonc tens aprés li revint li corrosion ou doi de la main, et il vint a moi,	And long time afterwards it returns the corruption or tooth of the hand, and it came to me,
et je li mis sus choses repercussives aprés la mundification dou cors, et ne pot cesser li corrosions;	and I put it on things reflective after the purification of the body, and the corruption did not cease.
et il vot que je li copasse la main, et je ne vou, que je avoie esperance de repercuter la matiere;	and he commanded me to cut off the hand, and I did not wish, if I had hope of reflection (of the matter).
et doutai ausi que se je tailloie sa main, qu’il ne morist,	He also feared that if I were to cut off his hand, he would die.
car li vertus de l’ome estoit foible; et il se despera toz, et revint en sa terre,	The virtues of a man were weak; he despaired completely and returned to his land.
et se hasta de coper sa main, et fut sanez;	and struck himself with a knife on the hand, and was healthy;
et je n’ai ceu conteit fuers que por ceu c’on faice autreteil, s’on en a mestier.	and I have not heard this story otherwise, unless there is a need for it.
Aucune fois vient aposteme en leu charnut, et demore si longement qu’il fait grant assemblee de bowe;	An abscess sometimes appears in the groin area and remains so long that it causes a great accumulation of pus;
et puis ront et perce, et en saut li bowe, et demoure li leus vuis, ausi com uns vasselz;	And then they run and pierce, and leap the bow, and keep the place firm, as a vassal.
et li cuir qui est desus est ausi subtilz com .i. drapelz deliiez,	The skin that is above is also as thin as a delicate cloth cut open.
et ne corront mie jusc’a l’os, ne jusc’au nerf, et telz maladie si est apelee «sain»,	and they do not pierce to the bone or to the nerve, and such a disease is called "wounded".
et n’est mie apelee «fistule»;	and it is not called "fistula".
mais s’elle est si alongie qu’elle viegne jusc’a l’os em parfont, si est apelee «fistule»;	but if it (the dislocation) is so long that it reaches the bone entirely, it is called "fistula".
et li cuire si est que tu cope celui cuir tout entor, et meismement quant il est subtilz, ausi com uns drapelz;	and you cook the meat entirely outside (of the body), similarly when it is thin, like a thin cloth.
et ne s’aert mie por sa corruption.	and it should not be avoided due to its corruption.
Et se tu as fiance que li cuirs s’aerde, et li corruption n’est mie en parfont,	If you have suspicion that the meat (flesh) is rotten, but the corruption is not in the bone,
et li cuir est espés de char, si le cure de clistere ensi:	And the skin is thick with flesh, if you cure it with a poultice like this:
regarde se li seins est grans, et li bowe qui en ist est de puant odor,	look to see if the breast is large and the sore in it smells bad,
adonques le clisterize de medicine egiptiaine qui est ensi faite:	Then prepare the Egyptian medicine poultice like this:
prenez aisil, et oile, et litargire, igalment, et metez cuire en .i. vassel au feu,	Take asafetida (or "aisil"), oil, and litharge, mix them equally, and cook in one vessel over the fire,
tant que li medicine soit rouge, et deviegne ausi espesse com miel;	until the medicine is red and becomes as thick as honey;
et puis pren de ceu selonc ta necessiteit, et le font en aigue et en miel,	and then take from this according to your need, and make it into water and honey,
et en clisterize lou sein, et estraint le pertus;	and anoint the breast and apply pressure (to the wound);
et laisse la medicine ens par .ij. houres, puis l’estrai en espreignant;	And leave the medicine in for two hours, then draw it out while waiting.
fai ce mout de fois, tant que li seins soit mondefiiez, et soit ostee li puor;	Do this many times, until the breast is softened and pus removed;
et aucune fois est clisterizeis d’aigue de cendres,	and sometimes it is cleansed with ash water.
quant ceste medicine n’est presens, et est que tu preignes cendres de fust de vigne, et giete aigue desus,	When this medicine is not present, and you take vine ash, pour water on it.
puis la coule, et en clisterize, tant que tu saiches que li seins est bien mondez;	then filter, and apply as a poultice, until you know that the wound is properly healed.
et se li malaides ne le puet soffrir, ne la medicine egiptiaine ne l’aigue de cendres,	but if the patient cannot tolerate it, or the Egyptian medicine or water of ashes,
si le clisterize d’aigue et de miel ou il ait un poc de litargire broiet;	if the poultice is made with water and honey and a little bit of litharge powder.
ou tu la clistirize de miel et de vin melleit, que li mielz ait proprieteit de mundifiier et de laver,	or you anoint it with honey and sweet wine, that the honey has properties of cleansing and washing.
et li vins fait aerdre le sain;	and the wine makes the wound heal.
et quant tu as ce fait, et tu as fiance que li seins est bien mundifiiez,	and when you have done this, and you are certain that the wound is well cleansed,
si le clisterize de ceu que fait naistre char en li,	if the anointing of these substances causes pus to form in them.
et est que tu preignes emplaustre diafinit, et le font avec oile roset et en vin;	And you are to prepare a plaster of definite consistency, and make it with rose oil and wine.
ou tu le clisterize d’aucunes medicines et d’oignemens, dont j’ai dit les proprietez ou traitier des oignemens;	And you are to apply a plaster of certain medicines and liniments, whose properties for treating wounds I have mentioned.
et se li pertus dou sein est petis, et li cainne dou clistere n’i puet entrer,	If the wound in the breast is small, and the linen cloth of the plaster cannot enter,
si l’eslarge d’un fer un poc, et met ens une tente de l’oignement egiptiein,	if the wound is about the width of a finger, and you place a tent of Egyptian liniment over it,
ou oignement basilicon, tant k’il soit eslargiez;	Apply basilicon ointment, as it is diluted.
et se li plaie est trop large, si la cout et i laisse tant soulement .i. leu ou li clistere puisse entrer,	and if the wound is too wide, cut it so that only one inch or a cleansing cloth can enter.
et se li pertus que giete bowe est au desus, si le cope ou plus bas leu que i est.	and if the ulcer that falls out is above, press it down or lower than it.
Car quant li bowe est en parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char;	For when the wound is fully open, do not let any pus enter.
et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues,	and if you cannot cover the wound beneath as you see,
si appareille en tel maniere que li bowe corre au plus bas leu que i est,	arrange it in such a way that the wound points downward as much as possible,
car quant li bowe est parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char	for when the wound is fully open, do not let any pus enter.
et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues,	And if you cannot cover the chest beneath as you see,
si apareille en teil maniere: que li bowe corre legierement aval, et n’i lassier rien de la bowe;	then tie it in this manner: let the sinew run lightly downwards without leaving anything of the sinew;
et pren medicines consolidatives por mettre sor le sein,	and take medicines that consolidate to put on the chest,
et estent sus .i. drapeil de lin que cuevre tout le sein;	and lay one linen cloth over it that covers the entire chest;
puis cope as forces endroit le pertus dou sein .i. poc plus large dou premier,	Then apply force to the breast wound, i.e., one slightly larger than the first,
pues estent oignement souef sus .i. autre drapel selonc la quantiteit dou pertus,	Then spread the liniment or other cloth according to the size of the wound,
et le met sus le pertus dou sein por aligier la bowe, et n’oster mie le grant drapeil fuers que aprés maint jor une fois;	and place the linen over the breast wound to straighten the blow, and do not remove the large cloth immediately but after several days.
et celui qui est sor le pertus dou sein, oste sovent por oster la bowe,	and one who is over the breast wound, often removes it in order to relieve the blow,
et saiches ceu que corra de la bowe, se c’est venin ou poc ou assez, ou digeste, ou indigeste;	And know what runs from the wound, whether it is poison or pus or enough, or digested, or undigested.
et pren warde se li patiens sent dolor ou nom, et s’il i a aposteme ou non,	And beware if the patient feels pain or not, and if there is an abscess or not.
et quant ta medicine s’est en teil maniere estendue et tu vois la nature que saut sus le pertus dou sein,	and when your medicine has been applied in this manner, and you see the nature jump over the breastbone,
si saiches que li seins s’aert ja, et aproche li santez;	if you know that the breasts have already begun to swell, approach the healthy;
et puis le deslie le matin, ou le tier jor, et quant tu delies la plaie,	And then dislocate it in the morning or the third day, when you dislocate the wound,
si chainge .i. autre drapeil, et renovele l’oignement.	Change one bandage and renew the ointment.
Et se li seins giete bowe indigeste aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie.	And if the breasts are swollen improperly after many days, know that the breasts do not heal.
Et se venins subtilz cort aprés lonc tens, si ne te desperer mie de la santeit,	And if subtle poisons cure for a long time, do not despair of health,
car li santez aproche. Car il i a homes cui tarde enjanremens de char en ses plaies, et de ces que font le contraire;	For the healing approaches. For there are men who delay the healing of flesh in their wounds, and from those who act contrary to this;
et se bowe indigeste saut dou sein aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie;	and bends improperly out of joint from the breast after many days, knowing that breasts do not dislocate;
et se li seins tarde d’aerdre, et est porloigniez, si ajoste medicines sechans moistes en substance et seches en vertut,	and if the breast takes a long time to heal and is swollen, apply drying medications that are moist in substance and dry in effect;
si com oignement diafinit, car il i a grant partie de vitriole, et c’est li derriene medicine;	Like an eggshell defined, for there is much part of glass [or vitreous material], and it is the final remedy.
pren oignement dyafinit, et le font avec oile roset, et l’arose de viel vin igal en substance;	Take the eggshell-like substance defined, make it with rose oil, and rise [beat] it with aged wine of equal consistency.
puis le confit et en use; et ceu meisme fait mielz cuit engroissiez,	then boil and use it; and the same is made better thickened,
quant oignemens dyafinit n’est presens,	when the eggshell-like substance defined is not present,
ou tu pren mirre et aloen et encens, et le broie, et le poudre sus le miel quant il est sor le feu;	Take myrrh, aloe, and incense, grind them together, and sprinkle the powder on honey while it is over the fire;
et puis en glue .i. drapel, et l’estent sor le sein, et aucune fois i aministre on aristologe longe,	Then dip one cloth and place it on the breast, and at times administer an Aristolochia longa.
et racines de lis celeste, qui est ausi com farine de veces et centoire;	and roots of celestial lily, which is like the flour and centaur.
et en use de simples ou de compostes: broie les, et en fai poudre, et met sus le miel que j’ai dit, et en use;	and use of simple or compound remedies: grind them, make powder, and sprinkle on the honey as I said, and use.
et se li cure est alongie, et n’est curez par ceste cure,	And if the patient is whole, and not treated by this cure,
adonc saiches que la corruptions est em parfont, et fait empression en l’os, ou as membres durs, ou as liemens;	then know that corruption enters completely, and makes an impression on the bone or hard members or ligaments;
si le cure de la cure de fistule, si com nos avons dit ci devant.	if the cure of the fistula (fistula treatment), as we said before.
de l’aposteme de l’ungle	of the abscess at the nailbed
Panarice est un aposteme que naist desoz l’ungle dou pouchiet de la main,	Pouria is an abscess that arises beneath the nail of the finger.
ou dou piet, ou par aventure naist en autres dois;	or in the toe, or by chance it arises in other fingers;
et quant il est envielliez, et on n’i prent garde, si i vient .i. aposteme chaus,	and when it becomes inflamed and is not cared for, one abscess follows another.
et corront et giete bowe tant qu’elle corront la racine de l’ungle, et par aventure la corront toute;	and they run and throw boiling water on it until it reaches the root of the nail, and by chance it burns all of it.
et vient li corrosions jusc’a l’os, tant qu’il i vient dolor puant, et est li chiés dou doi larges, et est li color fuxe.	And comes the corruption up to the bone, until pain smells, and the cheeks are wide, and the color turns red.
Quant tu le cures si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie,	When you treat it as we have said in the section above, and the treatment does not help at all.
si covient que tu copes a i. fer toute la superfluiteit qui est demoree de l’ungle,	If it doesn't work, you must cut off everything that is left of the nail.
puis cauterize la plaie aprés.	then cauterize the wound after.
Li cauteres est mout grans aide se li os est sains, et li ungle est sainne;	The cauteries are very great help if the bone is healthy, and the nail is healed.
et se li ungle apresse la char ens, et l’encomence a poindre, et la blece,	and if the nail under the skin begins to push through, and it starts to swell and blister,
si covient que tu mettes lou rait desoz l’ungle que point la char,	It is necessary that you put the salve under the nail so that it does not push through the skin.
et la boute en haut, et cope celi char subtilment et legierement,	and apply it to the top, and press down on the swelling gently and lightly,
et met sus le remenant de la char medicines ardans et corrosives por oster tout;	And place on top of the reset bone, hot and corrosive medicine for removing everything.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then heal with ointments until it heals.
Et se li corrosion est en l’os, si le cope, et trai fuer, car tant com li os corrumpus i est, si ne puet saner;	If the corrosion is in the bone, strike and draw it out, for as much as the bone is corrupted, it cannot heal.
et se tu vois le doi corrumpre, si le cope en .i. des nous si com il est devant dit,	and if you see the tooth corrupt, strike it in one blow as previously stated.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then heal while he is healthy;
et s’il est ferus, et boutez, et il sent grant dolor, si covient que tu le sainnes premier;	and if he is wounded, pierced, and feeling great pain, it is necessary that you drain him first;
puis cope l’ungle dou spatumile agut en taillant de travers desus,	then cut the nail with a sharp spatula from above,
et warde que li taille ne viegne jusc’a la char qui est desoz l’ungle, car li malaides sentiroit trop grant dolor;	And guard that the tip does not reach the bone which is beneath the nail, because the patient would feel too much pain.
et s’il avient, si met chose sus qui apaise.	If it happens, place something on top to soothe it.
la dolor dou sourdoit de la main	the pain in the hand is fading
Li dois ajostez qui naist en mains d’aucuns homes par aventure est toz charnus,	The fingers that spring up accidentally on some men are all fat.
et par aventure i a teil ou il a osses, et aucune fois i a ungle,	And by chance there is a tooth or bone, and sometimes a nail.
et aucun d’aus naissent en la racine de la jointure, ou li naissance est en aucuns nous des dois.	Sometimes they grow from the root of the joint, or their growth is in some of our fingers.
Cil qui naist en aucune nout dou doi ne se muet,	The one born in any nail of the finger does not move,
et cil qui naist a la jointure dou doi, par aventure se muet;	and the one born at the joint of the finger may move.
la taille de celui qui est charnus si est legiere, en teil maniere:	The girth (circumference) of one who is fat is light, in this manner:
taille le en sa racine d’un large spatumile.	The girth (circumference) of one who is fat is to be measured at the root with a broad spatula.
Cil qui naist en la racine de la jointure si est grief a curer: si te tien dou coper.	One born at the root of a joint is difficult to cure; keep it covered.
En celui qui naist ou doit au derrien nout, si covient que tu copes premier la char reondement jusc’a l’os,	In one who is born or should be at the navel, it is necessary that you cover the raw flesh around the bone,
puis cope l’os a une soie convenable a ceu, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then bind the bone with an appropriate splint, then heal it until it heals.
Li soudemens que vient as dois ensamble vient par naissance, ou par soudement de plaie, ou par arsure de feu, ou par semblans choses.	The dislocations that come to the joints all at once are due to birth, or from a blow to the wound, or by burning, or similar things.
Si couvient que tu copes celle soudeure, si que li doit repairent selonc lor formes naturelz;	If it is necessary to bind that dislocation, it should repair according to their natural forms;
puis met entre dous tentes ou drapelz moilliez en oile roset, qu’il ne se soudent;	then put between two cloths or dampened linen soaked in oil roset, so that they do not adhere together;
ou tu met entre dous pieces de plonc subtilz, tant que li leus soit soudez, si com il covient.	And you place between two thin pieces of wood, until the joints are soldered, as it should be.
Se soudemens vient a aucun de ses dois avec la paume, si cope celle sodure si com il covient.	If one of its two sides comes with the palm, then strike the splint as required.
Des vils	The peasants
Vis sont voinnes grosses envoloupees pleines de superfluitez melancoliouses, que vienent em plusors membres dou cors;	The veins are large and rounded, full of melancholic superfluidities that come in many members of the body.
et plus avient en jambes de ces qui vont a piet et qui travaillent et portent, que a autres.	And more often happens in the legs of those who walk and work and carry things, than in others.
Il covient donques que tu li aministres aucune fois espurgement de cole, et puis le saine de la basilique.	Therefore, you must sometimes administer cleansing with vinegar, and then apply the basilica (a medicinal ointment or paste made from powdered herbs).
Li cure de fer si est selonc .ij. manieres: l’une est c’on les cope, et traie on fuer le sanc noir;	The method of iron treatment is in two ways: one is to strike it and draw out black blood;
et li autre maniere si est que tu lieves la voinne, et la trai toute fuer.	And the other way is to open the vein and let all the blood flow out.
Li taille si est selonc ceste maniere: arose li premier la jambe d’aigue chaude mout fort, tant que li gros sans soit subtiliiez,	The thigh is prepared in this manner: first, warm the leg with very hot water, making sure that the flesh does not become too thin.
puis estrain la jambe dou malaide des desus la cuixe jusc’a la partie desoz le genoil;	then hold the patient's leg from above the knee to the part below the kneecap;
puis cope la voinne en .i. leu, ou en .ij. ou en .iij., d’une taille large,	then cut the vein in one, two, or three places, making a large incision.
puis eslieve et trair fuer le sanc noir a ta main, des l’un chief jusc’a l’autre, tant que tant de sans en isse com li vertus dou malaide puet soffrir;	Then extract and draw out the black blood from your hand, from one end to the other, as much as the strength of the patient can bear.
et puis la lie, et li comande qu’il se teigne de viandes enjanrant cole noire;	And tie it up, and instruct him to eat black meat with a bitter sauce.
et recomence l’evacuation et la sainie quant les voinnes sont plainnes, et nuist au malaide.	And begin the evacuation and purification again when the veins are full, which benefits the patient.
Li alevemens de li est selonc ceste maniere: reis la jambe dou malaide, s’il i a mout de poil,	The swelling is treated in this manner: raise the limb of the patient, if there is much hair.
puis le met ou bain, et li. arose la jambe d’aigue chaude tant qu’elle deviegne rouge, et enflent les voinnes;	Then immerse it (the affected part) in warm water, and raise the leg with hot water until it turns red, and the veins swell.
et se tu n’as point de baing, si le chaufe au feu, et puis le cope endroit la voinne dou lonc au chief dou genoil, ou en la partie desoz a la cheville;	And if there is no warm water, heat it with fire, and then apply it to the vein near the knee or in the part below the ankle.
puis aoevre le cuir a l’oncine, et escorche la voinne de chescune part, tant qu’ele apere quant on la sent;	Then scrape the skin with a knife at the edge, and peel off the vein from both sides until it appears when touched.
et on la voit rouge et noire, et quant elle entre ou cuir si semble ausi com une corde blainche;	It will appear red and black, and when it enters the skin it looks like a white cord.
puis boute le rait desoz, tant qu’ele soit alevee dou cuir, et puis la pent a l’oncine legier,	Then push the shoulder blade beneath, until it is raised to the skin, and then bend it at the little angle lightly.
puis le cope en .i. autre leu ensus iij. dois; puis escorche le cuir sus la voinne tant qu’ele apere,	Then strike one other place under four fingers; then cut the skin over the vein until it appears.
puis la lieve au rais, si com tu as fait, et la pent a un autre uncine, si com tu as fait premiers;	Then tie the shoulder again, just like you did before, and bend it at another little angle, just like you did first.
puis cope une autre taille, ou plusors se tu en as mestier, puis la lieve, et la cope au doi dou piet,	Then cut another piece, or more if necessary, then tie, and bend it to the thigh.
puis la trai et lieve jusc’a la seconde taille; puis l’estrai de taille en taille, tant qu’elle isse toute fuer, puis la cope;	Then draw and drain up to the second joint; then pull it out joint by joint, until it completely comes out, then break it.
et se tu ne la pues traire et lever, si i boute une aguille a tout .i. fil fort double,	and if you cannot draw and drain, push an awl with a single, very strong double thread through [it].
et la lie et la trai, et i boute desoz .i. rait, et torne ta main d’une part et d’autre, tant qu’il en isse;	and draw and pull it out, and push a rod under it, then turn your hand on both sides until it comes out.
et garde qu’elle ne cope, car s’elle cope, si ne la puet on traire ne lever, et en vient nuisement au malaide;	And keep it from bruising, for if it bruises, one cannot draw or lift it out, and this brings harm to the patient.
et quant tu l’as toute traite, si met sor le leu de la plaie laine moillie en vin et en oile roset; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you have treated it completely, place on the wound linen soaked in wine and rose oil; let it heal until it is healthy.
Et se li vis est contraite et torte et envoloupee ensamble, et ele n’est mie droite, si com nos avons dit,	And if the wounds are contracted, twisted, and entwined together, not straight as we have said,
si covient que tu la fendes tortement, mais ne la coper mie; et la trai si com nos avons devant dit.	You must cut it obliquely but do not cover it; pull it out as we have previously said.
Li forme dou fer dont on cope la vis si est corbes, et ne trenche mie, qu’il ne cope la voinne;	The shape of iron used to pierce the eye does not curve and does not cut, but only pierces the vein.
et est de grosse corbeure, car s’il estoit subtilz, si coperoit la voine, mais soit gros si com nos avons dit, et ci est li forme:	and is of large curve because if it is subtle, it would pierce the vein, but be large as we have said, and here is its shape:
De la voinne civile	From the civil vein
